\u003cstrong\u003eupstream\u003c/strong\u003e repository\u003c/a\u003e by adding it as a remote.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCreate a branch\u003c/strong\u003e for your changes.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eMake your changes.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePull in changes from upstream often to \u003ca href=\"https://help.github.com/articles/syncing-a-fork/\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003esync your fork\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/a\u003e so that merge conflicts will be less likely in your pull request.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://help.github.com/articles/creating-a-pull-request-from-a-fork/\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCreate a pull request\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/a\u003e when you are ready to propose your changes into the main project.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" solved\u003c/strong\u003e or the \u003cstrong\u003efeature added\u003c/strong\u003e, and this must be reported in the \u003cstrong\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://github.com/sofa-framework/sofa/blob/master/CHANGELOG.md\"\u003eCHANGELOG.md\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e file.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eCode must follow \u003cstrong\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://github.com/sofa-framework/sofa/blob/master/GUIDELINES.md\"\u003eour guidelines\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eCommit must build \u003cstrong\u003esuccessfully\u003c/strong\u003e on Jenkins for all steps (compilation + tests + examples).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eUnit Tests\u003c/strong\u003e are required for each new component or if an issue is fixed.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eExamples\u003c/strong\u003e (at least one) must be provided showing the new feature.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eManagement of pull pull-requests (BREAKING, major features) are reviewed by the \"Reviewers\" team and approved by the \"STC members\" team through a vote within a maximum period of 2 weeks.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eReviewing:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eMake sure the pull request is \u003cstrong\u003elabelized\u003c/strong\u003e and well assigned.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eControl that it follows \u003cstrong\u003eour rules\u003c/strong\u003e (defined above).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eTrack the \u003cstrong\u003estatus of each pull request\u003c/strong\u003e using the dedicated labels:\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\"pr: wip\" must be set if the PR has been created for a team work or if some fixes are needed (discussed in the comments).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\"pr: to review\" must be set if the PR is ready to be reviewed.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\"pr: ready\" must be set \u003cstrong\u003einstead of merge\u003c/strong\u003e if another PR merge is being built on the \u003ca href=\"https://www.sofa-framework.org/dash/?branch=origin/master\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eDashboard\u003c/a\u003e. It is used to delay the merge and avoid CI overflow.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eControl the builds\u003c/strong\u003e: Dashboard \u0026gt; Details in the pull request checks.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eMerge method: \u003cstrong\u003eprefer \"merge\"\u003c/strong\u003e or \"squash\" over \"rebase\".\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eRemember that:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eYou can \u003cstrong\u003eadd commits\u003c/strong\u003e in a pull request: see \u003ca href=\"https://help.github.com/articles/committing-changes-to-a-pull-request-branch-created-from-a-fork/\"\u003eGitHub documentation\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eIf the pull request contains out of scope commits (from a previous merge with master), \u003cstrong\u003econsider rebasing it\u003c/strong\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer nofollow\" href=\"https://camo.githubusercontent.com/c448e549a14ccb24bc78f3e8f9181bfacc606ef298e4c1000e4debdda90fcec7/68747470733a2f2f7777772e736f66612d6672616d65776f726b2e6f72672f77702d636f6e74656e742f75706c6f6164732f323032322f30362f4769744875622d50522d7265766965772d776f726b666c6f772e706e67\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://camo.githubusercontent.com/c448e549a14ccb24bc78f3e8f9181bfacc606ef298e4c1000e4debdda90fcec7/68747470733a2f2f7777772e736f66612d6672616d65776f726b2e6f72672f77702d636f6e74656e742f75706c6f6164732f323032322f30362f4769744875622d50522d7265766965772d776f726b666c6f772e706e67\" alt=\"PullRequestProcess\" style=\"width: 75%; If you are contributing code or documentation to the SOFA project, and using the git signed-off-by mechanism, you are agreeing to this certificate.  This DCO essentially means that:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eyou offer the changes under the same license agreement as the project, and\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eyou have the right to do that,\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eyou did not steal somebody else’s work.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe original DCO is available online : aria-labelledby="file-name-id-wide file-name-id-mobile" class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 eRvpKx"><div class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 cTsUqU js-snippet-clipboard-copy-unpositioned" data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Welcome</h1><a id="user-content-welcome" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Welcome" href="#welcome"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Welcome to the SOFA Community! Here is a brief summary of how it is structured:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>SOFA Users: people using SOFA by writing scenes or using the SOFA API.</li>
<li>SOFA Developers: people programming into SOFA, modifying the API, writing plugins.</li>
<li>SOFA Contributors: (awesome) people proposing their changes in SOFA code via pull-requests.</li>
<li>SOFA Reviewers: people reviewing and merging the pull-requests. This group is validated by the Scientific and Technical Committee (STC).</li>
<li>SOFA Consortium: research centers and companies willing to share the cost of development and maintenance of SOFA, hosted by Inria.</li>
<li>SOFA Consortium Staff: administrators of SOFA and its ecosystem. This group is directed by the Executive Committee (EC).</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">All SOFA Developers are gladly invited to the SOFA-dev meetings.<br>
They take place remotely every Wednesday at 10 a.m. CET and are animated by the SOFA Reviewers + the Consortium Staff.<br>
<a href="https://sympa.inria.fr/sympa/subscribe/sofa-dev" rel="nofollow">Subscribe to SOFA-dev mailing-list</a> to get the agenda, reports and conference room url.</p>
<p dir="auto">About the steering committees:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>SOFA Scientific and Technical Committee (STC): defines the technical roadmap twice a year, validate the contribution rules, the Reviewers team and discuss every technical point in SOFA.</li>
<li>SOFA Executive Committee (EC): decides on evolutions of the membership contract, the communication policy and the priorities of the Consortium.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">A more detailed definition of the committees is available <a href="https://www.sofa-framework.org/consortium/presentation/" rel="nofollow">in the SOFA website</a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Getting started</h1><a id="user-content-getting-started" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Getting started" href="#getting-started"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Please <strong>read carefully</strong> <a href="https://guides.github.com/activities/contributing-to-open-source/">the GitHub guide on Contributing to Open Source</a>. We also recommend you to check this <a href="https://help.github.com/categories/collaborating-with-issues-and-pull-requests/">more detailed documentation on issues and pull requests</a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Support - Discussion forum</h1><a id="user-content-support---discussion-forum" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Support - Discussion forum" href="#support---discussion-forum"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For any <strong>question</strong> (help needed, problem of understanding SOFA, announcements), create a topic on <a href="https://github.com/sofa-framework/sofa/discussions">the SOFA GitHub Discussions</a> and benefit from the feedback of the community.</p>
<p dir="auto">When creating a new topic, pay attention to some tips:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Check existing topics</strong> using the Search bar. Your question may have been answered already.</li>
<li><strong>Be clear</strong> about what your problem is: what was the expected outcome, what happened instead? Detail how someone else can recreate the problem.</li>
<li><strong>Additional infos</strong>: link to demos, screenshots or code showing the problem.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Issues</h1><a id="user-content-issues" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Issues" href="#issues"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For <strong>bug tracking</strong>, <strong>feature proposals</strong> and <strong>task management</strong>, create a <a href="https://github.com/sofa-framework/sofa/issues">SOFA issue</a>! There is nothing to it and whatever issue you are having, you are likely not the only one, so others will find your issue helpful, too. Issues labeled "discussion" are also used for larger topics: architecture, future of SOFA, long term dev, etc.</p>
<p dir="auto">Please <strong>DO NOT create an issue for questions or support</strong>. Use <a href="https://github.com/sofa-framework/sofa/discussions">the GitHub Discussions</a> instead.</p>
<p dir="auto">When creating an issue, pay attention to the following tips:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Check existing issues</strong>. What you are running into may have been addressed already.</li>
<li><strong>Set the right label</strong> to your issue among our label list or propose them in the description.</li>
<li><strong>Be clear</strong> about what your problem is: what was the expected outcome, what happened instead? Detail how someone else can recreate the problem.</li>
<li>If your issue reports a bug or any abnormal behavior in SOFA, a <strong>test highlighting the issue</strong> should be written and pull requested.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">For more information on issues, check out <a href="https://guides.github.com/features/issues/">this GitHub guide</a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Pull requests</h1><a id="user-content-pull-requests" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Pull requests" href="#pull-requests"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">If you are able to patch the bug or add the feature yourself – fantastic, make a pull request with the code! Be sure you have read any documents on contributing and you understand <a href="https://github.com/sofa-framework/sofa/blob/master/LICENCE.txt">the SOFA license</a>. Once you have submitted a pull request the maintainer(s) can compare your branch to the existing one and decide whether or not to incorporate (pull in) your changes.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Reminder - How to pull request (from GitHub documentation)</h3><a id="user-content-reminder---how-to-pull-request-from-github-documentation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Reminder - How to pull request (from GitHub documentation)" href="#reminder---how-to-pull-request-from-github-documentation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong><a href="http://guides.github.com/activities/forking/">Fork</a></strong> the repository and clone it locally.</li>
<li><a href="https://help.github.com/articles/configuring-a-remote-for-a-fork/">Connect your clone</a> to <a href="https://github.com/sofa-framework/sofa/">the original <strong>upstream</strong> repository</a> by adding it as a remote.</li>
<li><strong>Create a branch</strong> for your changes.</li>
<li>Make your changes.</li>
<li>Pull in changes from upstream often to <a href="https://help.github.com/articles/syncing-a-fork/"><strong>sync your fork</strong></a> so that merge conflicts will be less likely in your pull request.</li>
<li><a href="https://help.github.com/articles/creating-a-pull-request-from-a-fork/"><strong>Create a pull request</strong></a> when you are ready to propose your changes into the main project.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Start easy and simple</h3><a id="user-content-start-easy-and-simple" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Start easy and simple" href="#start-easy-and-simple"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For newcomers in the community, we regularly identify issues easy to tackle and to get started with, using a <a href="https://github.com/sofa-framework/sofa/issues?q=label%3A%22good+first+issue%22">label "<em>good first issue</em>"</a>. Choose one, solve it and create your first pull request!</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Rules</h3><a id="user-content-rules" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Rules" href="#rules"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Description must explain the <strong>issue solved</strong> or the <strong>feature added</strong>, and this must be reported in the <strong><a href="https://github.com/sofa-framework/sofa/blob/master/CHANGELOG.md">CHANGELOG.md</a></strong> file.</li>
<li>Code must follow <strong><a href="https://github.com/sofa-framework/sofa/blob/master/GUIDELINES.md">our guidelines</a></strong>.</li>
<li>Commit must build <strong>successfully</strong> on Jenkins for all steps (compilation + tests + examples).</li>
<li><strong>Unit Tests</strong> are required for each new component or if an issue is fixed.</li>
<li><strong>Examples</strong> (at least one) must be provided showing the new feature.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Management of pull requests</h3><a id="user-content-management-of-pull-requests" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Management of pull requests" href="#management-of-pull-requests"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Standard pull-requests are reviewed and approved by the "Reviewers" team.<br>
Major pull-requests (BREAKING, major features) are reviewed by the "Reviewers" team and approved by the "STC members" team through a vote within a maximum period of 2 weeks.</p>
<p dir="auto">Reviewing:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Make sure the pull request is <strong>labelized</strong> and well assigned.</li>
<li>Control that it follows <strong>our rules</strong> (defined above).</li>
<li>Track the <strong>status of each pull request</strong> using the dedicated labels:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>"pr: wip" must be set if the PR has been created for a team work or if some fixes are needed (discussed in the comments).</li>
<li>"pr: to review" must be set if the PR is ready to be reviewed.</li>
<li>"pr: ready" must be set <strong>instead of merge</strong> if another PR merge is being built on the <a href="https://www.sofa-framework.org/dash/?branch=origin/master" rel="nofollow">Dashboard</a>. It is used to delay the merge and avoid CI overflow.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Control the builds</strong>: Dashboard &gt; Details in the pull request checks.</li>
<li>Merge method: <strong>prefer "merge"</strong> or "squash" over "rebase".</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Remember that:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>You can <strong>add commits</strong> in a pull request: see <a href="https://help.github.com/articles/committing-changes-to-a-pull-request-branch-created-from-a-fork/">GitHub documentation</a>.</li>
<li>If the pull request contains out of scope commits (from a previous merge with master), <strong>consider rebasing it</strong>.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/c448e549a14ccb24bc78f3e8f9181bfacc606ef298e4c1000e4debdda90fcec7/68747470733a2f2f7777772e736f66612d6672616d65776f726b2e6f72672f77702d636f6e74656e742f75706c6f6164732f323032322f30362f4769744875622d50522d7265766965772d776f726b666c6f772e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/c448e549a14ccb24bc78f3e8f9181bfacc606ef298e4c1000e4debdda90fcec7/68747470733a2f2f7777772e736f66612d6672616d65776f726b2e6f72672f77702d636f6e74656e742f75706c6f6164732f323032322f30362f4769744875622d50522d7265766965772d776f726b666c6f772e706e67" alt="PullRequestProcess" style="width: 75%; max-width: 100%;" data-canonical-src="https://www.sofa-framework.org/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/GitHub-PR-review-workflow.png"></a></p><b>Workflow of a PR review</b>
<p dir="auto">For more information on forks and pull request, check out <a href="https://guides.github.com/activities/forking/">this GitHub guide</a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">SOFA Developer Certificate Of Origin (DCO)</h3><a id="user-content-sofa-developer-certificate-of-origin-dco" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: SOFA Developer Certificate Of Origin (DCO)" href="#sofa-developer-certificate-of-origin-dco"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">SOFA is using the <a href="https://www.kernel.org/doc/html/latest/process/submitting-patches.html#sign-your-work-the-developer-s-certificate-of-origin" rel="nofollow">mechanism of the linux project</a> to track and secure all issues related to copyrights: the Developper Certificate of Origin (DCO). If you are contributing code or documentation to the SOFA project, and using the git signed-off-by mechanism, you are agreeing to this certificate.  This DCO essentially means that:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>you offer the changes under the same license agreement as the project, and</li>
<li>you have the right to do that,</li>
<li>you did not steal somebody else’s work.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">The original DCO is available online : <a href="http://developercertificate.org" rel="nofollow">http://developercertificate.org</a></p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="Developer Certificate of Origin

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Annual development cycle</h1><a id="user-content-annual-development-cycle" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Annual development cycle" href="#annual-development-cycle"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
